---

## Introducción

En 2016 el periódico The Guardian publicó un informe con una comparativa interactiva de atletas competidoras del heptatlón en los juegos olímpicos Río del mismo año. La publicación es un sitio web HTML que incluye texto con visualizaciones embebidas escritas en lenguaje Javascript. Una de ellas es un selector desplegable con una lista de atletas y un gráfico comparativo de los resultados individuales para cada disciplina del heptatlón.

### La fuente
- **URL**: [https://www.theguardian.com/sport/ng-interactive/2016/aug/14/how-nafissatou-thiam-beat-the-odds-to-claim-the-heptathlon-gold-in-rio](https://www.theguardian.com/sport/ng-interactive/2016/aug/14/how-nafissatou-thiam-beat-the-odds-to-claim-the-heptathlon-gold-in-rio)
- **Publicado**: 14 agosto 2016

## Prompts

### Reescribir código

Usando Claude by Anthropic, primeramente pedimos reescriba el código para entender su funcionamiento.
> Rewrite the code using intuitive variables and function id names.

### Código javascript reescrito

```

//   1. Module Loader      — SystemJS-style module registry & executor

//   5. D3                 — select, voronoi, scale, line, color
//   6. roundPathCorners   — SVG path corner smoothing utility
//   7. Athlete Data       — per-discipline results + final rankings
//   8. Main Application   — visualization, table, interactions

            function Ib(a, b) {

            function animateCircleGrow(circles, athleteId, timestamp) {
                animationState[athleteId] ? animationState[athleteId].grow || (animationState[athleteId].grow = timestamp) : (animationState[athleteId] = { grow: timestamp });
                var elapsed = timestamp - animationState[athleteId].grow;
                elapsed < 150

                          return circle.setAttribute("r", circleRadius * easeOutFn(elapsed));
                      }),

                          animateCircleGrow(circles, athleteId, t);
                      }))
                    : (circles.forEach(function (circle) {
                          return circle.setAttribute("r", circleRadius * easeOutFn(150));
                      }),
                      delete animationState[athleteId].grow);
            }
            function animateCircleShrink(circles, athleteId, timestamp) {
                animationState[athleteId] ? animationState[athleteId].shrink || (animationState[athleteId].shrink = timestamp) : (animationState[athleteId] = { shrink: timestamp });

                          animateCircleShrink(circles, athleteId, t);
                      }))

                        (formatRunTime = function (rawValue, allValues) {
                            if (rawValue) {
                                var delta =
                                    rawValue -
                                    Math.min.apply(
                                        Math,
                                        toArray(
                                            allValues.filter(function (v) {
                                                return v;
                                            })
                                        )
                                    );
                                return delta > 0 ? rawValue + "s (+" + delta.toFixed(2) + ")" : rawValue + "s";
                            }
                            return "";
                        }),
                        (formatRunSeconds = function (totalSeconds) {
                            return (totalSeconds % 60).toFixed(2);
                        }),
                        (activeAthleteId = null),
                        (windowWidth = window.innerWidth),
                        (disciplines = [
                            {
                                name: "100m hurdles",
                                resMapper: function (a) {
                                    return a;
                                },
                                format: formatRunTime,
                                reverseScale: true,
                            },
                            {
                                name: "High jump",
                                resMapper: function (a) {
                                    return a;
                                },
                                format: function (v) {
                                    return v ? v + "m" : "";
                                },
                            },
                            {
                                name: "Shot put",
                                resMapper: function (a) {
                                    return a;
                                },
                                format: function (v) {
                                    return v ? v + "m" : "";
                                },
                            },
                            {
                                name: "200m run",
                                resMapper: function (a) {
                                    return a;
                                },
                                format: formatRunTime,
                                reverseScale: true,
                            },
                            {
                                name: "Long jump",
                                resMapper: function (a) {
                                    return a;
                                },
                                format: function (v) {
                                    return v ? v + "m" : "";
                                },
                            },
                            {
                                name: "Javelin throw",
                                resMapper: function (a) {
                                    return a;
                                },
                                format: function (v) {
                                    return v ? v + "m" : "";
                                },
                            },
                            {
                                name: "800m run",
                                resMapper: function (timeStr) {
                                    if (timeStr) {
                                        var parts = timeStr.split(":"),
                                            parsed = destructureIterator(parts, 2),
                                            mins = parsed[0],
                                            secs = parsed[1];
                                        return 60 * parseInt(mins) + parseFloat(secs);
                                    }
                                },
                                format: function (timeStr, allTimes) {
                                    if (timeStr) {
                                        var parts = timeStr.split(":"),
                                            parsed = destructureIterator(parts, 2),
                                            mins = parsed[0],
                                            secs = parsed[1],
                                            totalSecs = 60 * parseInt(mins) + parseFloat(secs),
                                            bestSecs = Math.min.apply(
                                                Math,
                                                toArray(
                                                    allTimes
                                                        .filter(function (t) {
                                                            return t;
                                                        })
                                                        .map(function (t) {
                                                            var p = t.split(":"),
                                                                parsed2 = destructureIterator(p, 2),
                                                                m = parsed2[0],
                                                                s = parsed2[1];
                                                            return 60 * parseInt(m) + parseFloat(s);
                                                        })
                                                )
                                            ),
                                            delta = totalSecs - bestSecs;
                                        return delta > 0 ? timeStr + " (+" + formatRunSeconds(delta) + ")" : timeStr;
                                    }
                                    return "";
                                },
                                reverseScale: !0,
                            },
                        ]),
                        (labelPadding = null),
                        (easeOutCubic = function (duration) {
                            return function (t) {
                                var c2 = -2 / (duration * duration * duration),
                                    c1 = 3 / (duration * duration),
                                    c0 = 1;
                                return c2 * t * t * t + c1 * t * t + c0;
                            };
                        }),
                        (animationState = {}),
                        (prevActiveId = null),
                        (circleRadius = 4),
                        (defaultAthleteIds = [finalResults[0]._id]),
                        (easeOutFn = null),
                        (axisMargin = 16),
                        (allResultCircles = null),
                        (allResultLabels = null),
                        (allDisciplineTitles = null),
                        (highlightAthlete = function (athleteId, forceUpdate) {
                            (athleteId !== activeAthleteId || forceUpdate) &&
                                !(function () {
                                    null !== activeAthleteId && unhighlightAthlete(activeAthleteId), (activeAthleteId = athleteId);
                                    var athlete = finalResults.find(function (r) {
                                        return r._id === athleteId;
                                    });
                                    (querySelector(".hepta-select").selectedIndex = finalResults.findIndex(function (r) {
                                        return r._id === athleteId;
                                    })),
                                        (querySelector(".hepta-select").className = athlete.medal
                                            ? "hepta-select hepta-select--" + athlete.medal
                                            : "hepta-select"),
                                        querySelector('.hepta-tr[data-id="' + athleteId + '"]').classList.add("hepta-hl");
                                    var line = querySelector('.hepta-line[data-id="' + athleteId + '"]');
                                    line && line.classList.remove("hepta-hidden"),
                                        querySelectorAll(".hepta-discipline").forEach(function (disciplineEl) {
                                            d3.select(disciplineEl)
                                                .selectAll(".hepta-result-group")
                                                .sort(function (a, b) {
                                                    var byActive = [athleteId].indexOf(a.e.identifier) - [athleteId].indexOf(b.e.identifier);
                                                    return 0 !== byActive
                                                        ? byActive
                                                        : ["bronze", "silver", "gold"].indexOf(a.e.medal) -
                                                              ["bronze", "silver", "gold"].indexOf(b.e.medal);
                                                });
                                        });
                                    var circles = querySelectorAll('.hepta-result-group[data-id="' + athleteId + '"] circle'),
                                        labels = querySelectorAll('.hepta-result-group[data-id="' + athleteId + '"] text');
                                    athlete.rank ? athlete.rank + "." : "";
                                    window.requestAnimationFrame(function (t) {
                                        animateCircleGrow(circles, athleteId, t);
                                    }),
                                        circles.forEach(function (c) {
                                            c.classList.add("hepta-hl");
                                        }),
                                        labels.forEach(function (lbl) {
                                            lbl.classList.remove("hepta-hidden");
                                        });
                                })();
                        }),
                        (unhighlightAthlete = function (athleteId) {
                            querySelector('.hepta-tr[data-id="' + athleteId + '"]').classList.remove("hepta-hl");
                            var line = querySelector('.hepta-line[data-id="' + athleteId + '"]');
                            line && line.classList.add("hepta-hidden");
                            var circles = querySelectorAll('.hepta-result-group[data-id="' + athleteId + '"] circle'),
                                labels = querySelectorAll('.hepta-result-group[data-id="' + athleteId + '"] text');
                            window.requestAnimationFrame(function (t) {
                                animateCircleShrink(circles, athleteId, t);
                            }),
                                circles.forEach(function (c) {
                                    c.classList.remove("hepta-hl");
                                }),
                                labels.forEach(function (lbl) {
                                    lbl.classList.add("hepta-hidden");
                                });
                        }),
                        (restoreDefaultHighlights = function () {
                            defaultAthleteIds.forEach(function (id) {
                                highlightAthlete(id, true);
                            });
                        }),
                        (renderDisciplineRow = function (discipline, svgWidth, rowHeight, yOffset, svgSelection) {
                            var disciplineGroup = svgSelection
                                    .append("g")
                                    .attr(
                                        "class",
                                        discipline.total ? "hepta-discipline hepta-discipline--total" : "hepta-discipline"
                                    ),
                                legendXPositions = windowWidth > 740 ? [axisMargin + labelPadding + 44, svgWidth - axisMargin - 48] : [svgWidth / 2 - 10, svgWidth / 2 + 10];
                            svgSelection
                                .append("text")
                                .attr("class", "hepta-legend")
                                .text("← worse")
                                .attr("x", legendXPositions[0])
                                .attr("y", axisMargin + rowHeight / 2 - 24)
                                .attr("text-anchor", "end"),
                                svgSelection
                                    .append("text")
                                    .attr("class", "hepta-legend")
                                    .text("better →")
                                    .attr("x", legendXPositions[1])
                                    .attr("y", axisMargin + rowHeight / 2 - 24)
                                    .attr("text-anchor", "begin"),
                                disciplineGroup
                                    .append("line")
                                    .attr("x1", axisMargin)
                                    .attr("x2", svgWidth - axisMargin)
                                    .attr("y1", yOffset + rowHeight / 2)
                                    .attr("y2", yOffset + rowHeight / 2)
                                    .attr("class", "hepta-axis");
                            var valueExtent = d3.extent(
                                    discipline.data.map(function (entry) {
                                        return discipline.resMapper(entry.pr.value);
                                    })
                                ),
                                scaleRange = discipline.reverseScale ? [svgWidth - axisMargin, axisMargin + labelPadding] : [axisMargin + labelPadding, svgWidth - axisMargin],
                                xScale = d3.scaleLinear().domain(valueExtent).range(scaleRange),
                                resultGroups = disciplineGroup
                                    .selectAll(".hepta-result-group")
                                    .data(discipline.data)
                                    .enter()
                                    .append("g")
                                    .attr(
                                        "class",
                                        discipline.total ? "hepta-result-group hepta-result-group--total" : "hepta-result-group"
                                    )
                                    .attr("data-id", function (entry) {
                                        return entry.e.identifier;
                                    })
                                    .attr("data-finished", function (entry) {
                                        return entry.pr.value;
                                    });
                            resultGroups.append("circle")
                                .attr("class", "hepta-result")
                                .attr("class", function (entry) {
                                    var cls = "hepta-result";
                                    return (
                                        entry.pr.value || (cls += " hepta-hidden"),
                                        entry.e.medal && (cls += " hepta-medal--" + entry.e.medal),
                                        cls
                                    );
                                })
                                .attr("cx", function (entry) {
                                    var x = entry.pr.value ? xScale(discipline.resMapper(entry.pr.value)) : 0;
                                    return x;
                                })
                                .attr("cy", yOffset + rowHeight / 2)
                                .attr("r", 4)
                                .attr("data-id", function (entry) {
                                    return entry.e.identifier;
                                });
                            resultGroups
                                .append("text")
                                .attr("class", "hepta-result-label hepta-hidden")
                                .text(function (entry) {
                                    return discipline.total
                                        ? entry.e.name + " (" + entry.e.country + ")"
                                        : discipline.format(
                                              entry.pr.value,
                                              discipline.data.map(function (d) {
                                                  return d.pr.value;
                                              })
                                          );
                                })
                                .attr("x", function (entry) {
                                    var offset = xScale(discipline.resMapper(entry.pr.value)) > svgWidth / 2 ? -8 : 8;
                                    "800m run" === discipline.name &&
                                        Math.abs(xScale(discipline.resMapper(entry.pr.value)) - svgWidth / 2) / svgWidth < 0.3 &&
                                        (offset = 0);
                                    var xPos = entry.pr.value ? xScale(discipline.resMapper(entry.pr.value)) + offset : 0;
                                    return xPos;
                                })
                                .attr("text-anchor", function (entry) {
                                    return "800m run" === discipline.name &&
                                        Math.abs(xScale(discipline.resMapper(entry.pr.value)) - svgWidth / 2) / svgWidth < 0.25
                                        ? "middle"
                                        : xScale(discipline.resMapper(entry.pr.value)) > svgWidth / 2
                                          ? "end"
                                          : "start";
                                })
                                .attr("y", yOffset + rowHeight / 2 + 32),
                                disciplineGroup
                                    .append("text")
                                    .text(discipline.name)
                                    .attr("y", yOffset + rowHeight / 2 - 8)
                                    .attr("x", 15)
                                    .attr("class", "hepta-discipline-title");
                        }),
                        (renderConnectingLines = function (svgWidth, rowHeight, linesGroup, svgSelection) {
                            var lineGenerator = d3
                                    .line()
                                    .x(function (pt) { return pt.x; })
                                    .y(function (pt) { return pt.y; })
                                    .defined(function (pt) { return pt.finished; }),
                                athletePoints = finalResults
                                    .map(function (athlete) { return athlete._id; })
                                    .map(function (id) {
                                        return svgSelection
                                            .selectAll('.hepta-result-group[data-id="' + id + '"]')
                                            .nodes()
                                            .filter(function (node) {
                                                return !node.classList.contains("hepta-result-group--total");
                                            })
                                            .map(function (node) {
                                                return {
                                                    _id: node.getAttribute("data-id"),
                                                    finished: node.getAttribute("data-finished"),
                                                    x: node.querySelector("circle").getAttribute("cx"),
                                                    y: node.querySelector("circle").getAttribute("cy"),
                                                };
                                            });
                                    }),
                                pathData = athletePoints.map(function (points) {
                                    return points.flatMap(function (pt, idx, arr) {
                                        if (arr[idx + 1]) {
                                            var nextPt = arr[idx + 1];
                                            return [
                                                pt,
                                                {
                                                    x: parseFloat(pt.x),
                                                    y: parseFloat(pt.y) + rowHeight / 2,
                                                    _id: pt._id,
                                                    finished: pt.finished && nextPt.finished,
                                                },
                                                {
                                                    x: parseFloat(nextPt.x),
                                                    y: parseFloat(pt.y) + rowHeight / 2,
                                                    _id: pt._id,
                                                    finished: pt.finished,
                                                },
                                            ];
                                        }
                                        return pt;
                                    });
                                });
                            linesGroup.selectAll(".hepta-line")
                                .data(pathData)
                                .enter()
                                .append("path")
                                .attr("d", function (pts) {
                                    return lineGenerator(pts)
                                        ? roundPathCorners(
                                              lineGenerator(pts)
                                                  .replace(/([A-Za-z])/g, " $1 ")
                                                  .replace(/,/g, " ")
                                                  .slice(1),
                                              20
                                          )
                                        : "";
                                })
                                .attr("data-id", function (pts) {
                                    return pts[0]._id;
                                })
                                .attr("class", "hepta-line hepta-hidden");
                        }),
                        (renderVoronoiOverlay = function (svgWidth, rowHeight, svgSelection) {
                            var voronoi = d3
                                    .voronoi()
                                    .extent([
                                        [0, 0],
                                        [svgWidth, 7 * rowHeight],
                                    ])
                                    .x(function (pt) { return pt.x; })
                                    .y(function (pt) { return pt.y; }),
                                finishedPoints = svgSelection
                                    .selectAll(".hepta-result-group")
                                    .nodes()
                                    .filter(function (node) {
                                        return node.getAttribute("data-finished");
                                    })
                                    .map(function (node) {
                                        var medalMatch = node
                                            .querySelector("circle")
                                            .classList.toString()
                                            .match(/medal--(.*)/);
                                        return (
                                            (medalMatch = medalMatch ? medalMatch[1] : null),
                                            {
                                                x: parseFloat(node.querySelector("circle").getAttribute("cx")),
                                                y: parseFloat(node.querySelector("circle").getAttribute("cy")),
                                                _id: node.getAttribute("data-id"),
                                                medal: medalMatch,
                                            }
                                        );
                                    })
                                    .sortBy(function (pt) {
                                        return ["bronze", "silver", "gold"].indexOf(pt.medal);
                                    })
                                    .immutableReverse()
                                    .uniqueWith(function (a, b) {
                                        return a.x === b.x && a.y === b.y;
                                    }),
                                voronoiPolygons = voronoi(finishedPoints).polygons();
                            svgSelection.selectAll(".hepta-voronoi")
                                .data(voronoiPolygons)
                                .enter()
                                .append("path")
                                .attr("d", function (polygon) {
                                    return "M" + polygon.join("L") + "Z";
                                })
                                .attr("class", "hepta-voronoi")
                                .attr("data-id", function (polygon) {
                                    return polygon.data._id;
                                });
                        }),
                        (renderAllDisciplines = function (svgWidth, rowHeight, svgSelection) {
                            var linesGroupSel = svgSelection
                                .selectAll(".hepta-lines")
                                .data([svgWidth])
                                .enter()
                                .append("g")
                                .attr("class", "hepta-lines");
                            disciplines.forEach(function (disc, discIndex) {
                                (disc.data = athleteDataByDiscipline[discIndex]),
                                    renderDisciplineRow(disc, svgWidth, rowHeight, axisMargin + rowHeight * discIndex, svgSelection);
                            }),
                                renderConnectingLines(svgWidth, rowHeight, linesGroupSel, svgSelection),
                                renderVoronoiOverlay(svgWidth, rowHeight, svgSelection);
                        }),
                        (window.init = function (config, options) {
                            iframeMessenger.enableAutoResize();
                            var topDiv = document.createElement("div");
                            topDiv.classList.add("hepta-top");
                            var nameHeading = document.createElement("h2");
                            nameHeading.classList.add("hepta-athlete-name");
                            var selectEl = querySelector(".hepta-select"),
                                tableBody = querySelector(".hepta-tbody");
                            finalResults.forEach(function (athlete) {
                                var row = document.createElement("tr");
                                (row.className = athlete.medal ? "hepta-tr hepta-tr--" + athlete.medal : "hepta-tr"),
                                    row.setAttribute("data-id", athlete._id);
                                var rankCell = document.createElement("td");
                                rankCell.className = "hepta-td hepta-td--rank";
                                var nameCell = document.createElement("td");
                                nameCell.className = "hepta-td hepta-td--athlete";
                                var scoreCell = document.createElement("td");
                                (scoreCell.className = "hepta-td hepta-td--score"),
                                    (scoreCell.innerHTML = athlete.score ? athlete.score : "-"),
                                    (rankCell.innerHTML = athlete.medal
                                        ? "<span class='hepta-table-medal hepta-medal--" + athlete.medal + "'></span>"
                                        : athlete.rank
                                          ? athlete.rank + "."
                                          : "DNF"),
                                    (nameCell.innerHTML = athlete.name + " (" + athlete.country + ")"),
                                    row.appendChild(rankCell),
                                    row.appendChild(nameCell),
                                    row.appendChild(scoreCell),
                                    row.addEventListener("mouseenter", function () {
                                        highlightAthlete(athlete._id);
                                    }),
                                    tableBody.appendChild(row);
                                var option = document.createElement("option");
                                option.setAttribute("value", athlete._id),
                                    (option.className = athlete.medal ? "hepta-option hepta-option--" + athlete.medal : "hepta-option"),
                                    (option.innerHTML = athlete.rank
                                        ? athlete.rank + ". " + (athlete.name + " (" + athlete.country + ")")
                                        : athlete.name + " (" + athlete.country + ")"),
                                    selectEl.appendChild(option);
                            }),
                                selectEl.addEventListener("change", function () {
                                    highlightAthlete(selectEl.value);
                                });
                            var vizContainer = querySelector(".hepta-viz-container");
                            window.addEventListener("resize", function () {
                                var newWidth = window.innerWidth;
                                Math.abs(newWidth - windowWidth) > 50 &&
                                    ((windowWidth = newWidth), (querySelector(".hepta-viz-container").innerHTML = ""), buildSvgVisualization(vizContainer, options), restoreDefaultHighlights());
                            }),
                                window.addEventListener("load", function () {
                                    buildSvgVisualization(vizContainer, options), restoreDefaultHighlights();
                                });
                        }),
                        (buildSvgVisualization = function (container, options) {
                            var svgEl = d3.select(container).append("svg").attr("class", "hepta-svg"),
                                TOTAL_HEIGHT = 735,
                                computedWidth = parseFloat(window.getComputedStyle(querySelector(".hepta-svg")).width);
                            (labelPadding = windowWidth < 740 ? 80 : 120),
                                renderAllDisciplines(computedWidth, TOTAL_HEIGHT / 7, svgEl),
                                (allResultCircles = querySelectorAll(".hepta-result")),
                                (allResultLabels = querySelectorAll(".hepta-result-label")),
                                (allDisciplineTitles = querySelectorAll(".hepta-discipline-title")),
                                (easeOutFn = easeOutCubic(150)),
                                querySelectorAll(".hepta-voronoi").forEach(function (voronoiEl) {
                                    var id = voronoiEl.getAttribute("data-id");
                                    voronoiEl.addEventListener("mouseenter", function () {
                                        highlightAthlete(id);
                                    }),
                                        voronoiEl.addEventListener("touchstart", function () {
                                            isTouchScrolling = false;
                                        }),
                                        voronoiEl.addEventListener("touchmove", function () {
                                            isTouchScrolling = true;
                                        }),
                                        voronoiEl.addEventListener("touchend", function () {
                                            isTouchScrolling || highlightAthlete(id);
                                        });
                                });
                        });
                },
            };
        });
})(function (bootstrapCallback) {
    bootstrapCallback();
});
//# sourceMappingURL=embed.js.map
```

### Replicar el documento

> https://interactive.guim.co.uk/2016/08/olympics-heptathlon-embeds/embed/embed.html Con el archivo embeds modificado, analiza la visualización interactiva y crea una réplica exacta de la gráfica usando web estática mobile first con HTML, sólo usando un documento HTML, no utilices frameworks. Permite agregar y editar atletas, nombres de atletas, los puntajes en cada disciplina, y agregar y editar disciplinas.

### Estructura de datos explicada

ORIGINAL_DISCIPLINES:  
- id: *identificador de disciplina*
- name: *nombre de la disciplina*
- unit: *unidad de medida utilizada en la disciplina*
- reverse: *si es true a menor valor mejor posición, si es false a mayor valor mejor posición*

ORIGINAL_ATHLETES:  
- id: *identificador de atleta*
- name: *nombre de atleta*
- country: *país de origen de atleta*
- score: *puntaje del atleta*
- medal: *medalla obtenida*
- scores: *es una estructura diccionario clave-valor con clave d0, d1, ... d6 disciplinas con sus valores*

### Estructura de datos generada (embebida en el HTML):
```
const ORIGINAL_DISCIPLINES = [
  { id: 'd0', name: '100m hurdles', unit: 's',  reverse: true  },
  { id: 'd1', name: 'High jump',    unit: 'm',  reverse: false },
  { id: 'd2', name: 'Shot put',     unit: 'm',  reverse: false },
  { id: 'd3', name: '200m run',     unit: 's',  reverse: true  },
  { id: 'd4', name: 'Long jump',    unit: 'm',  reverse: false },
  { id: 'd5', name: 'Javelin throw',unit: 'm',  reverse: false },
  { id: 'd6', name: '800m run',     unit: 'mm:ss', reverse: true },
];

const ORIGINAL_ATHLETES = [
  { id:'a1', name:'Nafissatou Thiam',        country:'BEL', score:6810, medal:'gold',

  { id:'a9', name:'Jennifer Oeser',          country:'GER', score:6401, medal:null,
    scores:{ d0:'13.69', d1:'1.77', d2:'15.33', d3:'24.99', d4:'6.55', d5:'53.70', d6:'2:14.84' }},

// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  STATE
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

let disciplines  = deepClone(ORIGINAL_DISCIPLINES);
let athletes     = deepClone(ORIGINAL_ATHLETES);
let activeId     = athletes[0].id;   // highlighted athlete

// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  UTILITIES
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

function deepClone(x) { return JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(x)); }

function uid() { return 'id_' + Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 9); }

/** Parse a value to a numeric float for scaling purposes */
function parseVal(str, unit) {
  if (!str) return null;
  if (unit === 'mm:ss') {
    const parts = String(str).split(':');
    if (parts.length < 2) return parseFloat(str);
    return parseInt(parts[0]) * 60 + parseFloat(parts[1]);
  }
  return parseFloat(str);
}

/** Format a value for display labels */
function fmtVal(str, unit, allVals) {
  if (!str) return '';
  if (unit === 'mm:ss') {
    const num  = parseVal(str, unit);
    const best = Math.min(...allVals.filter(v=>v!=null).map(v=>parseVal(v, unit)));
    const delta = num - best;
    return delta > 0 ? `${str} (+${(delta % 60).toFixed(2)})` : str;
  } else {
    const num  = parseFloat(str);
    const best = Math.min(...allVals.filter(v=>v!=null).map(v=>parseFloat(v)));
    const delta = num - best;
    if (unit === 'm') return delta > 0 ? `${str}m` : `${str}m`;
    return delta > 0 ? `${str}s (+${delta.toFixed(2)})` : `${str}s`;
  }
}

/** Linear scale: maps [dMin, dMax] → [rMin, rMax] */
function makeScale(dMin, dMax, rMin, rMax) {
  const dRange = dMax - dMin || 1;
  return v => rMin + (v - dMin) / dRange * (rMax - rMin);
}

// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  SVG HELPERS
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

const SVG_NS = 'http://www.w3.org/2000/svg';
function svgEl(tag, attrs = {}) {
  const el = document.createElementNS(SVG_NS, tag);
  for (const [k, v] of Object.entries(attrs)) el.setAttribute(k, v);
  return el;
}

// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  CHART RENDERING
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

const ROW_H    = 100;   // height per discipline row
const MARGIN_L = 12;
const MARGIN_R = 12;
const LABEL_PAD_DESKTOP = 96;  // left padding for axis start
const LABEL_PAD_MOBILE  = 72;

function isMobile() { return window.innerWidth < 640; }

function render() {
  renderSelect();
  renderChart();
  renderTable();
}

/* ── ATHLETE SELECT ── */
function renderSelect() {
  const sel = document.getElementById('athleteSelect');
  const prev = sel.value;
  sel.innerHTML = '';
  for (const a of athletes) {
    const opt = document.createElement('option');
    opt.value = a.id;
    opt.textContent = a.rank ? `${a.rank}. ${a.name} (${a.country})` : `${a.name} (${a.country})`;
    if (a.medal) opt.className = 'medal-' + a.medal;
    sel.appendChild(opt);
  }
  // restore or default
  const ids = athletes.map(a=>a.id);
  sel.value = ids.includes(prev) ? prev : (ids.includes(activeId) ? activeId : ids[0]);
  activeId = sel.value;
  updateSelectStyle();
}

function updateSelectStyle() {
  const sel = document.getElementById('athleteSelect');
  const a = athletes.find(a=>a.id===sel.value);
  sel.className = a && a.medal ? 'medal-'+a.medal : '';
}

/* ── CHART ── */
function renderChart() {
  const svg   = document.getElementById('chartSvg');
  svg.innerHTML = '';

  const lp = isMobile() ? LABEL_PAD_MOBILE : LABEL_PAD_DESKTOP;
  const W  = Math.max(svg.clientWidth || 340, 320);
  const numDiscs = disciplines.length;
  const H  = ROW_H * numDiscs;

  svg.setAttribute('viewBox', `0 0 ${W} ${H}`);
  svg.setAttribute('height', H);
  svg.style.minWidth = '300px';

  // For each discipline draw row
  disciplines.forEach((disc, di) => {
    const yMid = di * ROW_H + ROW_H / 2;
    const xMin = MARGIN_L + lp;
    const xMax = W - MARGIN_R - 12;

    // gather numeric values for this discipline
    const vals = athletes.map(a => parseVal(a.scores?.[disc.id], disc.unit));
    const validVals = vals.filter(v => v != null);
    if (!validVals.length) validVals.push(0, 1);
    const dMin = Math.min(...validVals);
    const dMax = Math.max(...validVals);
    const scale = disc.reverse
      ? makeScale(dMin, dMax, xMax, xMin)
      : makeScale(dMin, dMax, xMin, xMax);

    // Axis line
    const axisLine = svgEl('line', {
      x1: xMin, y1: yMid, x2: xMax, y2: yMid,
      class: 'axis-line'
    });
    svg.appendChild(axisLine);

    // Discipline title
    const title = svgEl('text', {
      x: 10, y: yMid - 8, class: 'disc-title',
      'dominant-baseline': 'auto'
    });
    title.textContent = disc.name;
    svg.appendChild(title);

    // Legend (← worse / better →) — only first row
    if (di === 0) {
      const tw = svgEl('text', { class:'legend-txt', 'text-anchor':'end' });
      tw.setAttribute('x', disc.reverse ? xMax + 30 : xMin - 4);
      tw.setAttribute('y', yMid - 24);
      tw.textContent = '← worse';
      svg.appendChild(tw);

      const tb = svgEl('text', { class:'legend-txt', 'text-anchor':'start' });
      tb.setAttribute('x', disc.reverse ? xMin - 4 : xMax - 30);
      tb.setAttribute('y', yMid - 24);
      tb.textContent = 'better →';
      svg.appendChild(tb);
    }

    // Dots + labels for each athlete
    athletes.forEach((a) => {
      const rawVal = a.scores?.[disc.id];
      const num = parseVal(rawVal, disc.unit);
      if (num == null) return;
      const cx = scale(num);
      const isActive = a.id === activeId;

      // dot
      const cls = ['result-dot', a.medal ? 'medal-'+a.medal : '', isActive ? 'hl' : ''].filter(Boolean).join(' ');
      const dot = svgEl('circle', {
        cx, cy: yMid, r: isActive ? 9 : 5,
        class: cls,
        'data-aid': a.id,
        'data-did': disc.id,
      });
      svg.appendChild(dot);

      // label
      if (rawVal) {
        const allDiscVals = athletes.map(b => b.scores?.[disc.id]).filter(Boolean);
        const labelTxt = fmtVal(rawVal, disc.unit, allDiscVals);
        const anchor = cx > W / 2 ? 'end' : 'start';
        const dx = cx > W / 2 ? -10 : 10;
        const lbl = svgEl('text', {
          x: cx + dx, y: yMid + 30,
          class: 'result-label' + (isActive ? ' hl' : ''),
          'text-anchor': anchor,
          'dominant-baseline': 'auto',
          'data-aid': a.id,
          'data-did': disc.id,
        });
        lbl.textContent = isActive ? labelTxt : '';
        if (isActive) lbl.textContent = disc.unit === 'm'
          ? rawVal + 'm'
          : disc.unit === 'mm:ss'
            ? rawVal
            : rawVal + 's';
        svg.appendChild(lbl);
      }
    });
  }); // end disciplines loop

  // ── CONNECTING PATHS ──────────────────────────────────────
  // Compute dot positions for active athlete across disciplines
  athletes.forEach(a => {
    const lp2 = isMobile() ? LABEL_PAD_MOBILE : LABEL_PAD_DESKTOP;
    const xMin0 = MARGIN_L + lp2;
    const xMax0 = W - MARGIN_R - 12;
    const isActive = a.id === activeId;

    const points = disciplines.map((disc, di) => {
      const num = parseVal(a.scores?.[disc.id], disc.unit);
      if (num == null) return null;
      const vals = athletes.map(b => parseVal(b.scores?.[disc.id], disc.unit)).filter(v=>v!=null);
      const dMin = Math.min(...vals), dMax = Math.max(...vals);
      const scale = disc.reverse
        ? makeScale(dMin, dMax, xMax0, xMin0)
        : makeScale(dMin, dMax, xMin0, xMax0);
      return { x: scale(num), y: di * ROW_H + ROW_H / 2, di };
    });

    // Build SVG path through non-null points (stepped horizontal midpoints)
    const nonNull = points.filter(p => p != null);
    if (nonNull.length < 2) return;

    let d = '';
    for (let i = 0; i < nonNull.length; i++) {
      const pt = nonNull[i];
      if (i === 0) {
        d += `M ${pt.x} ${pt.y}`;
      } else {
        const prev = nonNull[i-1];
        const midY = (prev.y + pt.y) / 2;
        // Horizontal step: go down to midpoint, across, then down to next dot
        d += ` L ${prev.x} ${midY} L ${pt.x} ${midY} L ${pt.x} ${pt.y}`;
      }
    }

    const medalClass = a.medal ? 'medal-'+a.medal : '';
    const path = svgEl('path', {
      d,
      class: ['conn-path', medalClass, isActive ? 'hl' : ''].filter(Boolean).join(' '),
      'data-aid': a.id,
    });
    svg.appendChild(path);
  });

  // ── VORONOI-LIKE HIT AREAS ─────────────────────────────────
  // Use transparent rects + event delegation for simplicity
  disciplines.forEach((disc, di) => {
    const lp3 = isMobile() ? LABEL_PAD_MOBILE : LABEL_PAD_DESKTOP;
    const xMin = MARGIN_L + lp3;
    const xMax = W - MARGIN_R - 12;
    const yTop = di * ROW_H;
    const yMid = di * ROW_H + ROW_H / 2;

    const vals = athletes.map(a => parseVal(a.scores?.[disc.id], disc.unit));
    const valid = vals.filter(v=>v!=null);
    if (!valid.length) return;
    const dMin = Math.min(...valid), dMax = Math.max(...valid);
    const scale = disc.reverse
      ? makeScale(dMin, dMax, xMax, xMin)
      : makeScale(dMin, dMax, xMin, xMax);

    // Place invisible hit rects near each athlete dot
    athletes.forEach(a => {
      const num = parseVal(a.scores?.[disc.id], disc.unit);
      if (num == null) return;
      const cx = scale(num);
      const hit = svgEl('rect', {
        x: cx - 22, y: yTop,
        width: 44, height: ROW_H,
        class: 'voronoi-cell',
        'data-aid': a.id,
      });
      hit.addEventListener('mouseenter', () => setActive(a.id));
      hit.addEventListener('click',      () => setActive(a.id));
      hit.addEventListener('touchstart', (e) => { e.preventDefault(); setActive(a.id); });
      svg.appendChild(hit);
    });
  });
}

/* ── TABLE ── */
function renderTable() {
  const tbody = document.getElementById('tableBody');
  tbody.innerHTML = '';
  // Sort by score desc (nulls last)
  const sorted = [...athletes].sort((a,b) => {
    if (a.score == null && b.score == null) return 0;
    if (a.score == null) return 1;
    if (b.score == null) return -1;
    return b.score - a.score;
  });

  sorted.forEach((a, i) => {
    const tr = document.createElement('tr');
    tr.dataset.aid = a.id;
    const medalClass = a.medal ? 'medal-'+a.medal : 'no-medal';
    tr.className = medalClass + (a.id === activeId ? ' hl' : '');

    const rankTd = document.createElement('td');
    rankTd.className = 'td-rank';
    if (a.medal) {
      const pip = document.createElement('span');
      pip.className = 'medal-pip ' + a.medal;
      rankTd.appendChild(pip);
    } else if (a.score != null) {
      rankTd.textContent = (i+1) + '.';
    } else {
      rankTd.textContent = 'DNF';
    }

    const nameTd = document.createElement('td');
    nameTd.innerHTML = `<span class="td-athlete">${a.name}</span><span class="td-country">${a.country}</span>`;

    const scoreTd = document.createElement('td');
    scoreTd.className = 'td-score';
    scoreTd.textContent = a.score != null ? a.score.toLocaleString() : '—';

    tr.appendChild(rankTd);
    tr.appendChild(nameTd);
    tr.appendChild(scoreTd);

    tr.addEventListener('mouseenter', () => setActive(a.id));
    tr.addEventListener('click',      () => setActive(a.id));
    tbody.appendChild(tr);
  });
}

// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  HIGHLIGHT LOGIC
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

function setActive(id) {
  if (activeId === id) return;
  activeId = id;

  // Update select
  const sel = document.getElementById('athleteSelect');
  sel.value = id;
  updateSelectStyle();

  // Update SVG dots
  document.querySelectorAll('.result-dot').forEach(el => {
    const isAct = el.dataset.aid === id;
    el.setAttribute('r', isAct ? 9 : 5);
    el.classList.toggle('hl', isAct);
  });

  // Update labels
  document.querySelectorAll('.result-label').forEach(el => {
    const isAct = el.dataset.aid === id;
    el.classList.toggle('hl', isAct);
    if (!isAct) el.textContent = '';
    else {
      // re-set text
      const disc = disciplines.find(d => d.id === el.dataset.did);
      const a    = athletes.find(a => a.id === id);
      if (disc && a) {
        const raw = a.scores?.[disc.id];
        if (raw) {
          el.textContent = disc.unit === 'm'
            ? raw + 'm'
            : disc.unit === 'mm:ss'
              ? raw
              : raw + 's';
        }
      }
    }
  });

  // Update connecting paths
  document.querySelectorAll('.conn-path').forEach(el => {
    el.classList.toggle('hl', el.dataset.aid === id);
  });

  // Update table rows
  document.querySelectorAll('#tableBody tr').forEach(tr => {
    tr.classList.toggle('hl', tr.dataset.aid === id);
  });
}

// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  EDIT PANEL
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

function renderEditPanel() {
  renderDiscEditor();
  renderAthletesEditor();
}

/* ── DISCIPLINES EDITOR ── */
function renderDiscEditor() {
  const container = document.getElementById('discEditor');
  container.innerHTML = '';
  disciplines.forEach((disc, i) => {
    const row = document.createElement('div');
    row.className = 'disc-row';
    row.draggable = true;
    row.dataset.idx = i;

    row.innerHTML = `
      <span class="drag-handle" title="Drag to reorder">⠿</span>
      <input type="text" class="disc-name-inp" value="${esc(disc.name)}" placeholder="Discipline name">
      <select class="disc-unit-sel">
        <option value="s"    ${disc.unit==='s'?'selected':''}>seconds (s)</option>
        <option value="m"    ${disc.unit==='m'?'selected':''}>metres (m)</option>
        <option value="mm:ss"${disc.unit==='mm:ss'?'selected':''}>min:sec</option>
      </select>
      <label style="font-size:.76rem;color:var(--muted);white-space:nowrap;">
        <input type="checkbox" class="disc-rev-chk" ${disc.reverse?'checked':''}> lower=worse
      </label>
      <button class="del-btn" title="Delete discipline">×</button>
    `;

    // events
    row.querySelector('.disc-name-inp').addEventListener('input', e => {
      disciplines[i].name = e.target.value;
    });
    row.querySelector('.disc-unit-sel').addEventListener('change', e => {
      disciplines[i].unit = e.target.value;
    });
    row.querySelector('.disc-rev-chk').addEventListener('change', e => {
      disciplines[i].reverse = e.target.checked;
    });
    row.querySelector('.del-btn').addEventListener('click', () => {
      disciplines.splice(i, 1);
      renderDiscEditor();
    });

    // drag-and-drop reordering
    row.addEventListener('dragstart', e => {
      e.dataTransfer.setData('text/plain', i);
      row.style.opacity = '.4';
    });
    row.addEventListener('dragend', () => { row.style.opacity = ''; });
    row.addEventListener('dragover', e => { e.preventDefault(); row.classList.add('drag-over'); });
    row.addEventListener('dragleave', () => { row.classList.remove('drag-over'); });
    row.addEventListener('drop', e => {
      e.preventDefault();
      row.classList.remove('drag-over');
      const from = parseInt(e.dataTransfer.getData('text/plain'));
      const to   = i;
      if (from === to) return;
      const [moved] = disciplines.splice(from, 1);
      disciplines.splice(to, 0, moved);
      renderDiscEditor();
    });

    container.appendChild(row);
  });
}

/* ── ATHLETES EDITOR ── */
function renderAthletesEditor() {
  const container = document.getElementById('athletesEditor');
  container.innerHTML = '';

  athletes.forEach((a, ai) => {
    const row = document.createElement('div');
    row.className = 'athlete-edit-row' + (a.medal ? ' medal-'+a.medal : '');

    // Scores inputs
    const scoresHTML = disciplines.map(disc => `
      <div class="score-field">
        <label>${esc(disc.name)}</label>
        <input type="text" class="score-inp" data-did="${disc.id}"
               value="${esc(a.scores?.[disc.id] ?? '')}"
               placeholder="${disc.unit === 'mm:ss' ? '2:09.54' : disc.unit === 'm' ? '6.51' : '12.84'}">
      </div>`).join('');

    row.innerHTML = `
      <div class="athlete-edit-header">
        <input class="inp-name" type="text" value="${esc(a.name)}" placeholder="Athlete name">
        <input class="inp-country" type="text" value="${esc(a.country)}" placeholder="NAT" maxlength="4">
        <input class="inp-score" type="number" value="${a.score ?? ''}" placeholder="Score">
        <select class="medal-select">
          <option value=""       ${!a.medal?'selected':''}>No medal</option>
          <option value="gold"   ${a.medal==='gold'?'selected':''}>🥇 Gold</option>
          <option value="silver" ${a.medal==='silver'?'selected':''}>🥈 Silver</option>
          <option value="bronze" ${a.medal==='bronze'?'selected':''}>🥉 Bronze</option>
        </select>
        <button class="athlete-del-btn" title="Remove athlete">×</button>
      </div>
      <div class="athlete-scores-grid">${scoresHTML}</div>
    `;

    // Bind header inputs
    row.querySelector('.inp-name').addEventListener('input', e => { athletes[ai].name = e.target.value; });
    row.querySelector('.inp-country').addEventListener('input', e => { athletes[ai].country = e.target.value.toUpperCase(); });
    row.querySelector('.inp-score').addEventListener('input', e => {
      const v = parseFloat(e.target.value);
      athletes[ai].score = isNaN(v) ? null : v;
    });
    row.querySelector('.medal-select').addEventListener('change', e => {
      athletes[ai].medal = e.target.value || null;
      row.className = 'athlete-edit-row' + (athletes[ai].medal ? ' medal-'+athletes[ai].medal : '');
    });
    row.querySelector('.athlete-del-btn').addEventListener('click', () => {
      athletes.splice(ai, 1);
      renderAthletesEditor();
    });

    // Bind score inputs
    row.querySelectorAll('.score-inp').forEach(inp => {
      inp.addEventListener('input', e => {
        const did = e.target.dataset.did;
        athletes[ai].scores = athletes[ai].scores || {};
        athletes[ai].scores[did] = e.target.value.trim() || null;
      });
    });

    container.appendChild(row);
  });
}

// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  ACTIONS
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

function addDiscipline() {
  const id = uid();
  disciplines.push({ id, name: 'New discipline', unit: 'm', reverse: false });
  // add empty score for all athletes
  athletes.forEach(a => { a.scores = a.scores || {}; a.scores[id] = null; });
  renderDiscEditor();
  renderAthletesEditor();
}

function addAthlete() {
  const id = uid();
  const scores = {};
  disciplines.forEach(d => { scores[d.id] = null; });
  athletes.push({ id, name: 'New Athlete', country: 'NAT', score: null, medal: null, scores });
  renderAthletesEditor();
  // scroll to new
  document.getElementById('athletesEditor').lastElementChild?.scrollIntoView({ behavior:'smooth' });
}

function applyChanges() {
  // recalculate ranks
  const withScore = athletes.filter(a => a.score != null).sort((a,b) => b.score - a.score);
  withScore.forEach((a, i) => { a.rank = i + 1; });
  athletes.filter(a => a.score == null).forEach(a => { a.rank = null; });

  if (!athletes.find(a => a.id === activeId)) {
    activeId = athletes[0]?.id || null;
  }

  render();
  // Keep edit panel open but scroll to chart
  document.getElementById('chartSvg').scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'start' });
}

function resetData() {
  if (!confirm('Reset all data to original Rio 2016 values?')) return;
  disciplines = deepClone(ORIGINAL_DISCIPLINES);
  athletes    = deepClone(ORIGINAL_ATHLETES);
  activeId    = athletes[0].id;
  render();
  renderEditPanel();
}

// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  BOOTSTRAP
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

function esc(str) {
  return String(str ?? '').replace(/&/g,'&amp;').replace(/"/g,'&quot;').replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/>/g,'&gt;');
}

// Set initial ranks
(function initRanks() {
  const withScore = athletes.filter(a => a.score != null).sort((a,b)=>b.score-a.score);
  withScore.forEach((a,i) => { a.rank = i+1; });
})();

// Wire up controls
document.getElementById('athleteSelect').addEventListener('change', e => {
  setActive(e.target.value);
  updateSelectStyle();
});

document.getElementById('editToggle').addEventListener('click', () => {
  const panel  = document.getElementById('editPanel');
  const toggle = document.getElementById('editToggle');
  const open   = panel.classList.toggle('open');
  toggle.classList.toggle('open', open);
  if (open) renderEditPanel();
});

document.getElementById('addDiscBtn').addEventListener('click', addDiscipline);
document.getElementById('addAthleteBtn').addEventListener('click', addAthlete);
document.getElementById('applyBtn').addEventListener('click', applyChanges);
document.getElementById('resetBtn').addEventListener('click', resetData);

// Responsive redraw
let resizeTimer;
window.addEventListener('resize', () => {
  clearTimeout(resizeTimer);
  resizeTimer = setTimeout(() => { renderChart(); }, 120);
});

// Initial render
render();
</script>
</body>
</html>

```
